Summary of Heat Exchanger Maximum Allowable Working Pressures :

For ASME UHX designs, the following values include MAWPs that 
consider the tubesheet, tubes, tube/tubesheet joint etc. These 
values were determined by iteration. Review the tubesheet analysis 
report for more information.

Internal Pressure Calculation Results : 
 
ASME Code, Section VIII, Division 2, 2015 
 
Spherical Head From 10 To 20 SA-533 B , Fig. 3.8 Curve at 750 °F 
 
Spherical Shell Calculation - Section 4.3.5.1 
 
Computed Minimum Required Thickness [t]: 
 = D/2*( exp( 0.5P/(S*E) )-1) + ci + co 
 = 86.116/2*(exp( 0.5 * 322.521/(37195.203 *1.000 ))-1) + 0.125 + 0.000 
 = 0.1871 + 0.125 + 0.000 = 0.3121 in. 
 
Computed Maximum Allowable Working Pressure [MAWP]: 
 = 2 * S * E * Ln( ( 2*t + D ) / D ) - Pliq 
 = 2 * 37195.2 * 1.000 * Ln( ( 2*0.662 + 86.116 )/86.116 ) - 2.521 
 = 1135.705 - 2.521 = 1133.1838 psig 
 
Computed Maximum Allowable Pressure New & Cold [MAPnc]: 
 = 2 * S * E * Ln( ( 2*t + D ) / D ) 
 = 2 * 37500.000 * 1.000 * Ln( ( 2*0.787 + 85.866 )/85.866 ) 
 = 1363.0558 psig 
 
Computed Stress Intensity at Design Pressure [S]: 
 = P * D^2 / ( E( Do^2 - D^2 ) ) 
 = 322.521 * 86.116^2/( 1.00 ( 87.441^2 - 86.116^2 ) ) 
 = 10402.379 psi 
 
Percent Fiber Elongation per Table 6.1 

[page 10]
PV Elite 2016 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L. 
FileName : 195001-CAL-001.00 
Internal Pressure Calculations : 
 
3 
 
 
 For Heads formed from Segments (75*tnom/Rf)*(1-Rf/Ro) 1.363 % 
 For one Piece doubly Curved Heads 100*ln(Db/(Df-2t)) 36.475 % 
 
Where Db is the blank diameter for one piece doubly curved surfaces [Db]: 
 = square root( 4 * Head Surface Area / 3.14159 ) 
 = square root( 4 * 12010.2/3.14159 ) 
 = 123.660 in. 
 
Cylindrical Shell From 20 To 30 SA-533 B , Fig. 3.8 Curve at 750 °F 
 
Cylindrical Shell Calculation - Section 4.3.3.1 
 
Computed Minimum Required Thickness [t]: 
 = 0.5*D*( exp( P/(S*E) )-1)+ci+co 
 = 0.5*85.093 *(exp( 325.845/(37195.203 *1.000 ))-1) + 0.125 + 0.000 
 = 0.3744 + 0.125 + 0.000 = 0.4994 in. Equation 4.3.1 
 
Computed Maximum Allowable Working Pressure [MAWP]: 
 = S * E * Ln( ( 2*t + D ) / D ) - Pliq 
 = 37195.203 * 1.000 * Ln( ( 2*0.741 + 85.093 )/85.093 ) - 5.845 
 = 642.350 - 5.845 = 636.5054 psig 
 
Computed Maximum Allowable Pressure New & Cold [MAPnc]: 
 = S * E * Ln( ( 2*t + D ) / D ) 
 = 37500.000 * 1.000 * Ln( ( 2*0.866 + 84.843 )/84.843 ) 
 = 757.9516 psig 
 
Computed Stress Intensity at Design Pressure [S]: 
 = P * D / ( E( Do - D ) ) 
 = 325.845 * 85.093/( 1.00 ( 86.575 - 85.093 ) ) 
 = 18705.5703 psi 
 

[page 11]
PV Elite 2016 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L. 
FileName : 195001-CAL-001.00

 Cylinders formed from Plate (50*tnom/Rf)*(1-Rf/Ro) 1.011 % 
 
Cylindrical Shell From 30 To 40 SA-533 B , Fig. 3.8 Curve at 750 °F 
 
Cylindrical Shell Calculation - Section 4.3.3.1 
 
Computed Minimum Required Thickness [t]: 
 = 0.5*D*( exp( P/(S*E) )-1)+ci+co 
 = 0.5*85.093 *(exp( 325.845/(37195.203 *1.000 ))-1) + 0.125 + 0.000 
 = 0.3744 + 0.125 + 0.000 = 0.4994 in. Equation 4.3.1 
 
Computed Maximum Allowable Working Pressure [MAWP]: 
 = S * E * Ln( ( 2*t + D ) / D ) - Pliq 
 = 37195.203 * 1.000 * Ln( ( 2*0.466 + 85.093 )/85.093 ) - 5.845 
 = 404.787 - 5.845 = 398.9424 psig 
 
Computed Maximum Allowable Pressure New & Cold [MAPnc]: 
 = S * E * Ln( ( 2*t + D ) / D ) 
 = 37500.000 * 1.000 * Ln( ( 2*0.591 + 84.843 )/84.843 ) 
 = 518.4380 psig 
 
Computed Stress Intensity at Design Pressure [S]: 
 = P * D / ( E( Do - D ) ) 
 = 325.845 * 85.093/( 1.00 ( 86.024 - 85.093 ) ) 
 = 29778.7676 psi

Elliptical Head From 40 To 50 SA-533 B , Fig. 3.8 Curve at 750 °F 
 
Head Calculation - Section 4.3.6 (and Section 4.3.7 for Ellipsoidal Head) 
 
Computed Minimum Required Thickness [t]: 
 tr = 0.3357 in. 
 t = tr + ci + co 
 = 0.3357 + 0.1250 + 0.0000 
 = 0.4607 in. - see below for the derivation 
 
For Elliptical heads: Compute [h, k, r,] per 4.3.7.1 and PTB-3 
 h = D/(2*Aspect Ratio) 
 = 84.843/(2*2.000 ) 
 = 21.211 in. 
 
 k = D/(2*h) 
 = 84.843/(2*21.211 ) 
 = 2.000 
 
 r = D( 0.5/k - 0.08 ) + ca 
 = 84.843 ( 0.5/2.000 - 0.08 ) + 0.125 
 = 14.548 in. 
 
 L = D(0.44 * k + 0.02 ) + ca 
 = 84.843 (0.44 *2.000 + 0.02) + 0.125 
 = 76.483 in. 
 
Step 3: Geometric Constants [BetaTh, PhiTh, Rth]: 
 Equations 4.3.8 to 4.3.11 as appropriate 
 t (corroded) and P for the calc.: t = 0.3357 in. P = 325.8451 psig 
 
 BetTh = acos[(0.5 * D - r)/(L - r)] 

[page 13]
PV Elite 2016 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L. 
FileName : 195001-CAL-001.00 
Internal Pressure Calculations : 
 
6 
 
 = acos[(0.5 * 85.093 - 14.548 )/(76.483 - 14.548 )] 
 = 1.1017 radians - Equation 4.3.8 
 
 PhiTh = sqrt( L * t ) / r 
 = sqrt( 76.483 * 0.336 )/14.548 
 = 0.3483 radians - Equation 4.3.9 
 
 PhiTh < BetaTh, Thus: 
 Rth = ( 0.5 * D - r ) / cos( BetaTh - PhiTh ) + r 
 = ( 0.5 * 85.093 - 14.548 )/cos( 1.102 - 0.348 ) + 14.548 
 = 52.9353 in. - Equation 4.3.10 
 
Step 4: Coefficients: Equations 4.3.12 to 4.3.15 [C1 and C2]: 
 r/D > 0.08, Thus: 
 C1 = 0.692 * ( r / D ) + 0.605 
 = 0.692 * ( 14.548/85.093 ) + 0.605 
 = 0.7233 - Equation 4.3.13 
 
 C2 = 1.46 - 2.6 * ( r/D ) = 1.46 - 2.6 * ( 14.548/85.093 ) 
 = 1.0155 - Equation 4.3.15 
 
Step 5: Pressure to produce knuckle elastic buckling [Peth]: 
 = C1 * Et * t ² / ( C2 * Rth * ( 0.5 * Rth - r )) 
 = 0.723 * 24597198 * 0.336 ²/ 
 ( 1.015 * 52.935 * ( 0.5 * 52.935 - 14.548 )) 
 = 3130.16 psig - Equation 4.3.16 
 
Step 6: Internal Pressure for max stress in knuckle equals yield [Py]: 
 C3 = Sy = 55693.602 psi (Not in the creep range - 4.3.6.1(f) ) 
 
 Py = C3 * t / ( C2 * Rth * ( 0.5 * Rth / r - 1 ) ) 
 = 55693.602 *0.336/(1.015 * 52.935 * ( 0.5 * 52.935/14.548 - 1 )) 
 = 424.578 psig - Equation 4.3.17 

[page 14]
PV Elite 2016 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L. 
FileName : 195001-CAL-001.00 
Internal Pressure Calculations : 
 
7 
 
 
Step 7: Value of Internal Press. resulting in buckling of knuckle [G and Pck]: 
 G = Peth/Py = 3130.156/424.578 = 7.372 
 
 G > 1, Thus: 
 Pck = ( ( 0.77508G - 0.20354G ² + 0.019274*G ³ ) / 
 ( 1 + 0.19014G - 0.089534G ² + 0.0093965*G ³ ) )Py 
 = ( ( 0.77508*7.372 -0.20354*7.372 ²+0.019274*7.372 ³)/ 
 ( 1+0.19014*7.372 -0.089534*7.372 ²+0.0093965*7.372 ³))*424.578 
 = 775.14 psig - Equation 4.3.19 
 
Step 8: Compute Allowable Pressure base on buckling of knuckle [Pak]: 
 = Pck/1.5 = 775.14/1.5 = 516.76 psig - Equation 4.3.21 
 
Step 9: Compute allowable pressure based on rupture of crown [Pac]: 
 = 2 * S * E / (L / t + 0.5 ) 
 = 2 * 37195.203 * 1.000/(76.483/0.336 + 0.5 ) 
 = 325.85 psig - Equation 4.3.22 
 
Step 10: Compute final pressure [Pa]: 
 = min( Pak, Pac ) = min(516.759 , 325.845 ) 
 = 325.85 psig - Equation 4.3.23: (same as original design pressure) 
 
Allowable pressure in Crown at given thickness [Pac]: 
 = 2 * S * E / (L / t + 0.5 ) 
 = 2 * 37195.203 * 1.000/(76.483/0.387 + 0.5 ) 
 = 375.277 psig 
 
Computed Maximum Allowable Pressure [MAWP]: 
 = MaxPressure - Pliq = 375.2775 - 5.845 = 369.4324 psig 
 
Computed Maximum Allowable Pressure New and Cold [MAPnc]: 

[page 15]
PV Elite 2016 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L. 
FileName : 195001-CAL-001.00 
Internal Pressure Calculations : 
 
8 
 
 = 501.0277 psig 
 
Computed Membrane Stress Intensity at Design Pressure [Sm]: 
 = 32295.766 psi 
 
Required Thickness of Straight Flange = 0.499 in.

 For Heads formed from Segments (75*tnom/Rf)*(1-Rf/Ro) 3.009 %

External Pressure Calculation Results : 
 
ASME Code, Section VIII, Division 2, 2015 
 
Spherical Head From Tsht to 20 Ext. Chart: CS-5 at 750 °F 
 
Maximum External Pressure per Div. 2 Section 4.4 
 
Elastic Hoop Compressive Membrane Failure Stress [Fhe]: 
 = 0.075 * Ey * ( t / Ro ) 
 = 0.075 * 24597198 * ( 0.662/43.720 ) 
 = 27950.102 psi 
 
Ratio of Elastic Hoop Compressive Membrane Failure Stress to Yield [Fr]: 
 = Fhe / Sy 
 = 27950.1 / 55693.6 
 = 0.502 
 
Predicted Buckling Stress [Fic]: 
 Since Fr <= 0.55, Fic = Fhe 
 = 27950.102 psi 
 
Allowable Circumferential Compressive Stress [Fha]: 
 Since Fr <= 0.55, Fha = Fhe/FS 
 = 27950.10/2.035 
 = 13733.845 psi 
 
Allowable External Pressure at the given Thickness [Pa]: 
 = 2 * Fha[t/Ro] 
 = 2 * 13733.845 [0.662/43.720 ] 
 = 416.158 psig 
 

[page 17]
PV Elite 2016 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L. 
FileName : 195001-CAL-001.00

Cylindrical Shell From 20 to 30 Ext. Chart: CS-5 at 750 °F 
 
Maximum External Pressure per Div. 2 Section 4.4 
 
Determine Parameter [Mx]: 
 = L / sqrt( Ro * t ) 
 = 240.158/sqrt( 43.287 * 0.741 ) 
 = 42.400 
 
Compute the Factor [Ch]: 
 Since Mx > 13 and Mx < 2 * (Do/t) 
0.94 , Ch = 1.12 * Mx -1.058 
 = 1.12 * 42.400 -1.058 
 = 0.0213 
 
Elastic Hoop Compressive Membrane Failure Stress [Fhe]: 
 = 1.6 * Ch * Ey * ( t / Do ) 
 = 1.6 * 0.021 * 24597198 * ( 0.741/86.575 ) 
 = 7161.130 psi 
 
Ratio of Elastic Hoop Compressive Membrane Failure Stress to Yield [Fr]: 
 = Fhe / Fy 
 = 7161.1/55693.6 
 = 0.129 
 
Predicted Buckling Stress [Fic]: 
 Since Fr <= 0.552, Fic = Fhe 
 = 7161.130 psi 
 
Compute the Factor of Safety [FS]: 
 Since Fic [7161.13 ] < 0.55 * 55693.60 , FS = 2

 = 9337.4 / 55693.6 
 = 0.168 
 
Predicted Buckling Stress [Fic]: 
 Since Fr <= 0.55, Fic = Fhe 
 = 9337.411 psi 
 
Compute the Factor of Safety [FS]: 
 Since Fic [9337.41 ] < 0.55 * 55693.60 , FS = 2 
 
Allowable Circumferential Compressive Stress [Fha]: 
 Since Fr <= 0.55, Fha = Fhe/FS 
 = 9337.41/2.000 
 = 4668.706 psi 
 
Allowable External Pressure at the given Thickness [Pa]: 
 = 2 * Fha[t/Ro] 
 = 2 * 4668.706 [0.387/76.422 ] 
 = 47.261 psig

Minimum Required Thickness for Shear [HreqS]: 
 = 1/(4 * Mu) * (Do/(0.8 * S)) * [Ps - Pt] + Cats + Catc 
 = 1/(4 * 0.286 ) * (83.03 /(0.8 * 26496.80 )) * [-15.00 - 320.00 ] + 0.250 
 = 1.3982 in. 
 
UHX-12.5.1 Step 1: 
 
Compute the Equivalent Outer Tube Limit Circle Diameter [Do]: 
 = 2 * ro + dt 
 = 2 * 41.2032 + 0.6250 = 83.031 in. 
 

[page 31]
PV Elite 2016 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L.

Determine the Basic Ligament Efficiency for Shear [mu]: 
 = (p - dt) / p 
 = (0.875 - 0.625 ) / 0.875 = 0.286 
 
UHX-12.5.2 Step 2 : 
 
Compute the Ratio [Rhos]: 
 = Ds / Do (Configurations a, b, c) 
 = 85.0925 / 83.0314 = 1.0248 
 
Compute the Ratio [Rhoc]: 
 = Dc / Do (Configurations a, e, f) 
 = 86.1161 / 83.0314 = 1.0372 
 
Moment on Tubesheet due to Pressures (Ps, Pt) [Mts]: 
 = Do ²/16 * [(Rhos-1)*(Rhos ²+1)* Ps - (Rhoc-1) * (Rhoc ²+1) * Pt ] 
 = 83.031 ²/16 * [ (1.025 - 1) * (1.025 ² + 1) * -14.997 - 
 (1.037 - 1) * (1.037 ² + 1) * 320.000 ] 
 = -10961.7852 psig*in. ² 
 
UHX-12.5.3 Step 3, Determination of Effective Elastic Properties : 
 
Compute the Ratio [rho]: 
 = ltx / h = 0.0000 / 6.4429 = 0.0000 ( must be 0 <= rho <= 1 ) 
 
Compute the Effective Tube Hole Diameter [d*]: 
 = max( dt - 2tt*( Et/E )( St/S )( rho ), dt - 2tt) 
 = max( 0.6250 -2*0.0650 *(24847414 /24248608 )* 
 ( 13889 /26496 )*(0.000 ), 0.6250 -2*0.0650 ) 
 = 0.6250 in. 
 
Compute the Effective Tube Pitch [p*]:

ASME TS Calc : tsh

 = 0.8750 / sqrt( 1 - 4 * min( 290.94 *1.000 , 4*83.031 *0.875 ) 
 (3.141* 83.031 ²) ) 
 = 0.8995 in. 
 
Compute the Effective Ligament Efficiency for Bending [mu*]: 
 = (p* - d*) / p* = (0.8995 - 0.6250 ) / 0.8995 = 0.30515 
 
E*/E and nu* for Triangular pattern from Fig. UHX-11.3. 
 h/p = 7.363326 ; mu* = 0.305147

UHX-12.5.4 Step 4: 
 
Compute Shell Coefficient [betaS]: 
 = (( 12 * (1-nus ²))^0.25 )/((Ds + ts) * ts ) ½ 
 = (( 12 * (1 - 0.30 ²) )^0.25 ) / (( 85.0925 + 0.7411 ) * 0.7411 ) ½ 
 = 0.2279 1/in.

 = betaS * Es * ts ³ / ( 6 * (1 - rnus ²) ) 
 = 0.228 * 24597214 * 0.741 ³ / ( 6 * (1 - 0.300 ²) ) 
 = 417997.1250 psig*in. ²

 = (6*Ds*ks)/h ³ * (1 + h*betaS + *(h*betaS) ²/2 ) 
 = 6* 85.093 * 417997.125/6.443 ³ * ( 1 + 6.443 *0.228 + 1.078 ) 
 = 2829983.0000 psig

 = 85.093 ²/( 4 * 24597214 * 0.741 ) * ( 1 - 0.3 /2 ) 
 = 0.0000844023 in./psi 
 
Calculate Parameter [OmegaS]: 
 = rhos * ks * betaS * deltaS( 1 + h * betaS ) 
 = 1.0248 * 417997.12 * 0.2279 * 0.000084 ( 1 + 6.4429 * 0.2279 )

 ------------------------------------------------------------------ 
 Step 11, The Cylinder-to-Tubesheet Juncture is Overstressed.

UHX-12.5.1 Step 1: 
 
Compute the Equivalent Outer Tube Limit Circle Diameter [Do]: 
 = 2 * ro + dt 
 = 2 * 41.2032 + 0.6250 = 83.031 in. 
 
Determine the Basic Ligament Efficiency for Shear [mu]: 
 = (p - dt) / p 
 = (0.875 - 0.625 ) / 0.875 = 0.286 
 
UHX-12.5.2 Step 2 : 
 
Compute the Ratio [Rhos]: 
 = Ds / Do (Configurations a, b, c) 
 = 85.0925 / 83.0314 = 1.0248 
 
Compute the Ratio [Rhoc]: 
 = Dc / Do (Configurations a, e, f) 
 = 86.1161 / 83.0314 = 1.0372 
 
Moment on Tubesheet due to Pressures (Ps, Pt) [Mts]: 
 = Do ²/16 * [(Rhos-1)*(Rhos ²+1)* Ps - (Rhoc-1) * (Rhoc ²+1) * Pt ] 
 = 83.031 ²/16 * [ (1.025 - 1) * (1.025 ² + 1) * 320.000 - 
 (1.037 - 1) * (1.037 ² + 1) * -14.997 ] 
 = 7515.8843 psig*in. ²

Compute the Ratio [rho]: 
 = ltx / h = 0.0000 / 6.4429 = 0.0000 ( must be 0 <= rho <= 1 ) 
 
Compute the Effective Tube Hole Diameter [d*]: 
 = max( dt - 2tt*( Et/E )( St/S )( rho ), dt - 2tt) 
 = max( 0.6250 -2*0.0650 *(24847414 /24248608 )* 
 ( 13889 /26496 )*(0.000 ), 0.6250 -2*0.0650 ) 
 = 0.6250 in. 
 
Compute the Effective Tube Pitch [p*]: 
 = p / sqrt( 1 - 4 * min( AL * CNV_factor, 4*Do*p)/(Pi * Do ²) ) 
 = 0.8750 / sqrt( 1 - 4 * min( 290.94 *1.000 , 4*83.031 *0.875 ) 
 (3.141* 83.031 ²) ) 
 = 0.8995 in. 
 
Compute the Effective Ligament Efficiency for Bending [mu*]: 
 = (p* - d*) / p* = (0.8995 - 0.6250 ) / 0.8995 = 0.30515

 = (( 12 * (1-nus ²))^0.25 )/((Ds + ts) * ts ) ½

Determine Shell Coefficient [Lambdas]:

 = 6* 85.093 * 417997.125/6.443 ³ * ( 1 + 6.443 *0.228 + 1.078 )

 = 1.0248 * 417997.12 * 0.2279 * 0.000084 ( 1 + 6.4429 * 0.2279 ) 
 = 20.3412 in. ²

 = (( 12 * (1 - nuc ²) )^0.25 )/((Dc + tc) * tc )^0.5 
 = (( 12 * (1 - 0.30 ²) )^0.25 )/((86.1161 + 0.6624 ) * 0.6624 )^0.5

 = 313939.5938 psig*in. ²

 = 6*86.116 *313939.594/(6.443 ³) * ( 1 + 6.443 *0.240 + 1.193 )

 = A / Do = 87.4409 / 83.0314 = 1.0531 
 
Determine Coefficient [F]: 
 = (1 - nu*)/E* * ( Lambdas + Lambdac + E * ln(K) ) 
 = (1 - 0.35 )/6981298 * ( 2829983 + 2267117 + 
 24248608 * ln(1.05 ) ) 
 = 0.5911 

[page 53]
PV Elite 2016 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L. 
FileName : 195001-CAL-001.00 
ASME TS Calc : tsh 
 
46 
 
 
UHX-12.5.6 Step 6: 
 
Moment Acting on Unperforated Tubesheet Rim [M*] 
 = Mts + OmegaC * Pt - OmegaS * Ps 
 = -3615.339 + 62.604 * 320.000 - 413.765 * 320.000 
 = -7592.6099 psig*in. ² 
 
UHX-12.5.7 Step 7: 
 
Maximum Bending Moment acting on Periphery of Tubesheet [Mp]: 
 = ((M*) - Do ²/32 * F * (Ps - Pt) ) / (1 + F) 
 = ((-7592.61 ) - 83.031 ²/32 * 0.591 * (320.00 - 320.00 ) ) / (1 + 0.59 ) 
 = -4772.0723 psig*in. ² 
 
Maximum Bending Moment acting on Center of Tubesheet [Mo]: 
 = Mp + Do²/64 * (3 + rnu*)(Ps - Pt) 
 = -4772.07 + 83.031 ²/64 * (3 + 0.350 )(320.00 - 320.00 ) 
 = -4772.0723 psig*in. ² 
 
Maximum Bending Moment acting on Tubesheet [M]: 
 = Max( abs(Mp), abs(Mo) ) 
 = Max( abs(-4772.072 ), abs(-4772.072 ) ) 
 = 4772.0723 psig*in. ² 
 
UHX-12.5.8 Results for Step 8: 
 
Tubesheet Bending Stress at Original Thickness: 
 = 6 * M / ( (mu*) * ( h - hg') ² ) 
 = 6 * 4772.072 / ( (0.3051 ) * ( 6.4429 - 0.0000 ) ² ) 
 = 2260.4009 psi

PV Elite 2016 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L. 
FileName : 195001-CAL-001.00 
ASME TS Calc : tsh

The Allowable Tubesheet Bending Stress [SigmaAll]: 
 = 2 * S = 2 * 26496.80 = 52993.60 psi 
 
Tubesheet Bending Stress at Final Thickness [Sigma]: 
 = 6 * M / ( (mu*) * ( h - hg') ² 
 = 6 * 278.685 / ( (0.3051 ) * ( 1.3306 - 0.0000 )² 
 = 58.9243 psi 
 
Required Tubesheet Thickness, for Bending Stress [HreqB]: 
 = H + CATS + CATC = 1.3306 + 0.1250 + 0.1250 = 1.5806 in. 
 
Required Tubesheet Thickness for Given Loadings (includes CA) [Hreq]: 
 = Max( HreqB, HreqS ) = Max( 1.5806 , 0.2500 ) = 1.5806 in. 
 
UHX-12.5.9 Step 9: 
 
 abs(Ps - Pt) = abs(320.00 - 320.00 ) = 0.000 psig 
 
Shear Stress check [Tau_limit]: 
 = 3.2 * S * MU * h / Do 
 = 3.2 * 26496.80 * 0.286 * 6.443 / 83.03 = 1879.81 psig 
 
Average Shear Stress at the Outer Edge of Perforated Region [Tau]: 
 = 1/(4* Mu) * (Do/h) * [Ps - Pt] 
 = 1/(4*0.286)*(83.03/6.44)*[320.00-320.00]psi 
 = 0.00 psi

 = Ds ² / (4 * ts * (Ds + ts) ) * Ps 
 = 85.0925 ² / (4 * 0.7411 * (85.0925 + 0.7411 ) ) * 320.000

 = 9105.711 psi

 = 6*ks/ts ² * ( betaS * P's + 6*(1 - rnu*) / (E*) * 
 Do/h ³ * (1 + h * betaS/2) * (Mp + Do ² / 32 * (Ps - Pt) )) 
 = 6*417997.12 /0.741 ² * [ 0.228 *0.03 + 6*(1 - 0.350 )/6981298 *

 = 0.398

 = 0.968 - 0.125 
 = 0.843 in.

 = min( (( t + te )/tn)^0.35, 1 ) 
 = min( (( 0.662 + 0.000 )/0.843 )^0.35, 1 ) 
 = min( 0.919 , 1 ) 
 = 0.919

 = 9999999.000

Computed Minimum Required Thickness [t]: 
 = 0.5*D*( exp( P/(S*E) )-1)+ci+co 
 = 0.5*22.314 *(exp( 322.349/(14788.799 *1.000 ))-1) + 0.125 + 0.000 
 = 0.2459 + 0.125 + 0.000 = 0.3709 in. Equation 4.3.1 
 
Computed Maximum Allowable Working Pressure [MAWP]: 
 = S * E * Ln( ( 2*t + D ) / D ) - Pliq 
 = 14788.799 * 1.000 * Ln( ( 2*0.843 + 22.314 )/22.314 ) - 0.000 
 = 1077.209 - 0.000 = 1077.2095 psig 
 
Nozzle Minimum Thickness per Table 4.5.2 
 Min. required Nozzle Neck Thickness + c : 0.453 in. 11.515 mm 
 
Nozzle Calculations per Section 4.5: Internal Pressure Case: 
 
Nozzle Material Factor [frn]: 
 = min[Sn/S, 1] 
 = min[14788.8/37195.2 , 1] 
 = 0.398 
 
Thickness of Nozzle [tn]: 
 = thickness - corrosion allowance 
 = 0.968 - 0.125 
 = 0.843 in. 
 
Shell Diameter to Thickness ratio [D/t]: 
 = Di/t 
 = 86.116/0.662 
 = 130.006 must be less than 400. 
 
Effective Pressure Radius [Reff]: 
 = Di/2 + corrosion allowance 

[page 77]
PV Elite 2016 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L. 
FileName : 195001-CAL-001.00 
Nozzle Calcs. : T2 
 
70 
 
 = 85.866/2 + 0.125 
 = 43.058 in. 
 
Effective Length of Vessel Wall [LR]: 
 = min( sqrt( Reff * t ), 2 * Rn ) 
 = min( sqrt( 43.058 * 0.662 ), 2 * 11.157 ) 
 = 5.341 in. 
 
Intermediate value [Cn]: 
 = min( (( t + te )/tn)^0.35, 1 ) 
 = min( (( 0.662 + 0.000 )/0.843 )^0.35, 1 ) 
 = min( 0.919 , 1 ) 
 = 0.919 
 
Intermediate value [Cp]: 
 = 9999999.000 
 
Effective Nozzle Wall Length Outside the Vessel [LH]: 
 = min( t + te + Fp * sqrt( Rn*tn ), Lpr1 + t ) 
 = min(0.662+0.000+0.919*sqrt(11.157*0.843),11.811+0.662) 
 = 3.481 in. 
 
Effective Vessel Thickness [teff]: 
 = t + (( A5 * frp ) / LR ) 
 = 0.662+((0.000*1.00)/5.341) 
 = 0.662 in. 
 
Compute Areas A1-A43 (No Pad) or A1-A5 (With Pad) : 
 
Area Contributed by the Vessel Wall [A1]: 
 = t * LR 
 = 0.662 * 5.341 
 = 3.538 in ² 

[page 78]
PV Elite 2016 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L. 
FileName : 195001-CAL-001.00 
Nozzle Calcs. : T2 
 
71 
 
 
Area Contributed by the Nozzle Outside the Vessel Wall [A2]: 
 = tn * LH 
 = 0.843 * 3.481 
 = 2.935 in ² 
 
Area Contributed by the Outside Fillet Weld [A41]: 
 = 0.5 * Leg41 
2 
 = 0.5 * 0.394 2 
 = 0.078 in ² 
 
The total area contributed by A1 through A43 [AT]: 
 = A1 + frn( A2 + A3 ) + A41 + A42 + A43 
 = 3.538+0.398(2.935+0.000)+0.078+0.000+0.000 
 = 4.782 in ² 
 
Nozzle Radius for Force Calculation [Rxn]: 
 = tn / ln[1 + tn/Rn ] 
 = 0.843/ln[ 1 + 0.843/11.157 ] 
 = 11.573 in. 
 
Shell Radius for Force Calculation [Rxs]: 
 = teff / ln[ 1 + teff/Reff ] 
 = 0.662/ln[ 1 + 0.662/43.058 ] 
 = 43.388 in. 
 
Allowable Local Primary Membrane Stress [Sallow]: 
 = 1.5 * S * E 
 = 1.5 * 37195.203 * 1.000 
 = 55792.8 psi 
 
Determine Force acting on the Nozzle [fN]:

PV Elite 2016 Licensee: INGENIERIA Y TECNICAS DE MONTAJE LOINTEK S.L.

 = P * Rxn * LH 
 = 322.349 * 11.573 * 3.481 
 = 12986.6 lb. 
 
Determine Force acting on the Shell [fS]: 
 = P * Rxs * ( LR + tn )/2 
 = 322.349 * 43.388 * ( 5.341 + 0.843 )/2 
 = 43242.3 lb. 
 
Discontinuity Force from Internal Pressure [fY]: 
 = ( P * Rxs * Rnc )/2 
 = ( 322.349 * 43.388 * 11.157 )/2 
 = 78021.9 lb. 
 
Area Resisting Internal Pressure [Ap]: 
 = ( fS + fY + fN )/P 
 = ( 43242.3 + 78021.9 + 12986.6 )/322.349 
 = 416.5 in ²

 = Sallow /( 2 * Ap/AT - Rxs/(2 * teff ) ) 
 = 55792.805/( 2 * 416.476/4.782 - 43.388/(2*0.662 ) ) 
 = 394.5 psig

 = 2 * 37195.203 * [0.662/43.388 ] 
 = 1135.7 psig

 = 3364.375 < or = to 37195.203 Weld Size is OK

 = tn / ln[1 + tn/Rn ] 
 = 1.687/ln[ 1 + 1.687/10.313 ]

 = teff / ln[ 1 + teff/Reff ] 
 = 0.741/ln[ 1 + 0.741/42.546 ] 
 = 42.916 in. 
 
Allowable Local Primary Membrane Stress [Sallow]: 
 = Shell Fha Value

 = 3580.6 psi

 = 14.997 * 42.916 ( 5.615 + 1.687 ) 
 = 4700.0 lb.

 = 14.997 * 42.916 * 10.313 
 = 6637.6 lb.

 = 0.5*D*( exp( P/(S*E) )-1)+ci+co 
 = 0.5*20.626 *(exp( 320.000/(14788.799 *1.000 ))-1) + 0.125 + 0.000 
 = 0.2256 + 0.125 + 0.000 = 0.3506 in. Equation 4.3.1

 = S * E * Ln( ( 2*t + D ) / D ) - Pliq 
 = 14788.799 * 1.000 * Ln( ( 2*1.687 + 20.626 )/20.626 ) - 0.000 
 = 2240.524 - 0.000 = 2240.5237 psig

 = min[Sn/S, 1] 
 = min[14788.8/37195.2 , 1] 
 = 0.398

 = thickness - corrosion allowance 
 = 1.812 - 0.125 
 = 1.687 in.

 = Di/t 
 = 85.093/0.741

 = Di/2 + corrosion allowance 
 = 84.843/2 + 0.125 
 = 42.546 in.

 = min( sqrt( Reff * t ), 2 * Rn ) 
 = min( sqrt( 42.546 * 0.741 ), 2 * 10.313 ) 
 = 5.615 in.

 = min[1.5t,te] + sqrt( Rn * tn ) 
 = min[1.5*0.741 , 0.000 ] + sqrt( 10.313 * 1.687 ) 
 = 4.171 in.

 = Lpr1 
 = 11.811 
 = 11.811 in.

 = 4.912 in.

 = Max( 0.196 , 0.245 ) 
 = 0.245

131 
 
 
 Sd1 = Max( 0.8*Sd1, Sd1User ) 
 = Max( 0.113 , 0.142 ) 
 = 0.142

 = Ct * hn 
x where Ct = 0.020, x = 0.75 and hn = Structural Height (ft.) 
 = 0.020 * ( 14.8015 0.75 ) 
 = 0.151 seconds

 = ( 1/Natural Frequency ) = ( 1/33.000 ) 
 = 0.030

 = Minimum Value of (1.700 * 0.151 , 0.030 ) per 12.8.2 
 = 0.030

 = 0.3 * Sds * W * I 
 = 0.3 * 0.245 * 764638 * 1.25 
 = 70251.125 lb.

 = Ct * hn 
x where Ct = 0.020, x = 0.75 and hn = Structural Height (ft.) 
 = 0.020 * ( 9.1519 0.75 ) 
 = 0.105 seconds

Fundamental Period (1/Frequency) [T]: 
 = ( 1/Natural Frequency ) = ( 1/33.000 ) 
 = 0.030 
 
Check the Value of T which is the smaller of Cu*Ta and T: 
 = Minimum Value of (1.700 * 0.105 , 0.030 ) per 12.8.2 
 = 0.030

 = 0.3 * Sds * W * I 
 = 0.3 * 0.245 * 382320 * 1.25 
 = 35125.629 lb.

Formulas and Substitutions for Horizontal Vessel Analysis: 
 
Note: Wear Plate is Welded to the Shell, k = 0.1 
 
The Computed K values from Table 4.15.1: 
 K1 = 0.1066 K2 = 1.1707 K3 = 0.8799 K4 = 0.4011 
 K5 = 0.7603 K6 = 0.0529 K7 = 0.0529 K8 = 0.3405 
 K9 = 0.2711 K10 = 0.0581 K1* = 0.1923 K6p = 0.0379 
 K7p = 0.0379 
 
The suffix 'p' denotes the values for a wear plate if it exists. 
 
Note: Dimension a is greater than or equal to Rm / 2. 
 
Moment per Equation 4.15.3 [M1]: 
 = -Q*a [1 - (1- a/L + (R ²-h2 ²)/(2a*L))/(1+(4h2)/3L)] 
 = -208956*6.36[1-(1-6.36/41.73+(3.565 ²-1.778 ²)/ 
 (2*6.36*41.73))/(1+(4*1.78)/(3*41.73))] 
 = -240809.1 ft.lb. 
 
Moment per Equation 4.15.4 [M2]: 
 = Q*L/4(1+2(R ²-h2 ²)/(L ²))/(1+(4h2)/( 3L))-4a/L 
 = 208956*41.7/4(1+2(3.565 ²-1.778 ²)/(41.73 ²))/(1+(4*1.778)/ 
 (3*41.732))-4*6.36/41.73 
 = 755519.0 ft.lb. 
 
Longitudinal Stress at Top of Shell (4.15.6) [Sigma1]: 
 = P * Rm/(2t) - M2/(pi*Rm ²t) 
 = 320.000 * 42.779/(2*0.466 ) - 9066228/(pi*42.8 ²*0.466 ) 
 = 11314.99 psi

Longitudinal Stress at Bottom of Shell (4.15.7) [Sigma2]: 
 = P * Rm/(2t) + M2/(pi * Rm ² * t) 
 = 320.000 * 42.779/(2 * 0.466 ) + 9066228/(pi * 42.8 ² * 0.466 ) 
 = 18089.49 psi 
 
Longitudinal Stress at Top of Shell at Support (4.15.10) [Sigma*3]: 
 = P * Rm/(2t) - M1/(K1*pi*Rm ²t) 
 = 320.000*42.779/(2*0.466)--2889709.8/(0.1066*pi*42.8 ²*0.466) 
 = 24829.04 psi 
 
Longitudinal Stress at Bottom of Shell at Support (4.15.11) [Sigma*4]: 
 = P * Rm/(2t) + M1/(K1* * pi * Rm ² * t) 
 = 320.000*42.779/(2*0.466)+-2889709.8/(0.1923*pi*42.8 ²*0.466) 
 = 9089.34 psi 
 
Maximum Shear Force in the Saddle (4.15.5) [T]: 
 = Q(L-2a)/(L+(4*h2/3)) 
 = 208956 ( 41.73 - 2 * 6.36 )/(41.73 + ( 4 * 1.78/3)) 
 = 137412.1 lb. 
 
Shear Stress in the shell no rings, not stiffened (4.15.14) [tau2]: 
 = K2 * T / ( Rm * t ) 
 = 1.1707 * 137412.11/( 42.7790 * 0.4656 ) 
 = 8077.37 psi 
 
Decay Length (4.15.22) [x1,x2]: 
 = 0.78 * sqrt( Rm * t ) 
 = 0.78 * sqrt( 42.779 * 0.466 ) 
 = 3.481 in. 
 
Circumferential Stress in shell, no rings (4.15.23) [sigma6]:

 = -K5 * Q * k / ( t * ( b + X1 + X2 ) )

Effective reinforcing plate width (4.15.1) [B1]: 
 = min( b + 1.56 * sqrt( Rm * t ), 2a ) 
 = min( 19.69 + 1.56 * sqrt( 42.779 * 0.466 ), 2 * 76.378 ) 
 = 26.65 in. 
 
Wear Plate/Shell Stress ratio (4.15.29) [eta]: 
 = min( Sr/S, 1 ) 
 = min( 37195.203/37195.203 , 1 ) 
 = 1.0000 
 
Circumferential Stress at wear plate (4.15.26) [sigma6,r]: 
 = -K5 * Q * k / ( B1( t + eta * tr ) ) 
 = -0.7603 * 208956 * 0.1/( 26.647 ( 0.466 + 1.000 * 0.591 ) ) 
 = -564.50 psi 
 
Circ. Comp. Stress at Horn of Saddle, L>=8Rm (4.15.27) [sigma7,r]: 
 = -Q/(4(t+eta*tr)b1) - 3*K7*Q/(2(t+eta*tr) ²) 
 = -208956/(4(0.466 + 1.000 * 0.591 )26.647 ) - 
 3 * 0.053 * 208956/(2(0.466 + 1.000 * 0.591 ) ²) 
 = -16708.56 psi

Calculation of Axial Load, Intermediate Values and Compressive Stress 
 
Effective Baseplate Length [e]: 
 = ( Bplen - Clearance ) / ( Nribs - 1) 
 = ( 78.3465 - 1.0 )/( 7 - 1 ) = 12.8911 in. 
 
Baseplate Pressure Area [Ap]: 
 = e * Bpwid / 2 
 = 12.8911 * 19.6850/2 = 126.8807 in ² 
 
Axial Load [P]: 
 = Ap * Bp 
 = 126.9 * 135.49 = 17190.7 lb. 
 
Area of the Rib and Web [Ar]: 
 = ( Bpwid - Clearance - Webtk ) * Ribtk + e/2 * Webtk 
 = ( 19.685 - 1.0 - 0.984 ) * 0.984 + 12.8911/2 * 0.984 
 = 23.766 in ² 
 
Compressive Stress [Sc]: 
 = P/Ar 
 = 17190.7/23.7661 = 723.3315 psi

Bolt Area Calculation per Dennis R. Moss 
 
Bolt Area Requirement Due to Longitudinal Load [Bltarearl]: 
 = 0.0 (QO > QL --> No Uplift in Longitudinal direction) 
 
Bolt Area due to Shear Load [Bltarears]: 
 = Fl / (Stba * Nbolts) 
 = 50323.38/(25000.00 * 8.00 ) 
 = 0.2516 in ²

Bolt Area due to Transverse Load 
 
Moment on Baseplate Due to Transverse Load [Rmom]: 
 = B * Ft + Sum of X Moments 
 = 5.51 * 17562.81 + 0.00 
 = 96745.28 ft.lb. 
 
Eccentricity (e): 
 = Rmom / QO 
 = 1160943/167744.59 
 = 6.92 in. < Bplen/6 --> No Uplift in Transverse direction 
 
Bolt Area due to Transverse Load [Bltareart]: 
 = 0 (No Uplift) 
 
Required Area of a Single Bolt [Bltarear]: 
 = max[Bltarearl, Bltarears, Bltareart] 
 = max[0.0000 , 0.2516 , 0.0000 ] 
 = 0.2516 in ²
